Betel Nut and Dioscorea Pill: Treats damp phlegm and ear deafness.

Ingredients: 2 taels of rhubarb, 2 taels of scutellaria, 4 taels each of the vine and talc, and 2 taels of betel nut. Grind these into a powder, mix with water to make pills the size of tung seeds. Take ten pills at a time, then add ten more, taken with warm water.

Kidney Fire Powder: Treats kidney deficiency and ear deafness.

Ingredients: 1 tael of magnetite, calcined and soaked in vinegar seven times, ground to a powder; 1 tael of processed aconite, skin removed; 1 tael of cynomorium; 1 tael of Sichuan pepper, eyes and closed mouths removed, lightly stir-fried to induce sweating. Grind these into a powder. For each dose, use one pig's kidney, remove sinew and membrane, finely chop, and mix with 1 fen each of green onion and chives, 1 qian of the powdered medicine, and a pinch of salt. Wrap in ten layers of damp paper and steam over ashes until done, chew thoroughly without hollowing out, followed by thin congee. Effects after ten days. (The formula from "Precious Mirror" does not include cynomorium.)

Cistanche Pill: Treats kidney deficiency ear deafness, or wind evil entering the meridians, causing tinnitus.

Ingredients: Cistanche soaked in wine and roasted; 1 tael each of cornelian cherry flesh, stone lotus, and sweet flag; 1 tael of dodder seeds soaked in wine, steamed, and roasted; 1 tael of notopterygium; deer antler removed of hair, steamed in wine, then roasted; 1 tael of dendrobium; magnetite fire calcined, soaked in vinegar, and water-ground; processed aconite.

Additional: 7 scorpions, toxins removed; half a character of musk. Grind these ingredients into a powder, mix with honey to form pills the size of tung seeds. Each dose consists of 100 pills, taken with empty and any salt or wine soup.[100p]

Yi Shen San - for treating kidney deficiency and hearing loss.
Ingredients:

  • Magnetite, Ba Ji Tian, and Chuan Jiao (each one tael)
  • Shi Chang Pu and Chen Xiang (each five qian)

Sang Piao Xiao Soup
Treats hearing loss due to deficiency.
Ten pieces of roasted Sang Piao Xiao, Angelica, white atractylodes soaked in rice wash and stir-fried, cinnamon, white Poria peeled, prepared Aconite, Schizonepeta, fire-calcined Magnetite, vinegared and quilled Acorus, roasted Rehmannia, each one tael; large yellow ground, stir-fried; five qian each of Asarum, Chuanxiong, and Peony root; chew the above (with mouth) to taste, taking three qian per dose. First boil one pig kidney in three cups of water, extract one cup of juice, remove the kidney, add the herbs, and simmer to seventy percent concentrated; strain and take warm before meals.

Sheep Kidney Pill
Treats hearing loss due to kidney deficiency or fatigue reducing vital energy, cerebrovascular deficiency, kidney energy not descending, or persistent ear ringing.

Dihuang Pills: Treats labor-induced deafness.

Wax Ball Pills (from San Yin): Treats lung deficiency-induced deafness.
Two taels of white poria, three taels of roasted yam, one tael and five qian of roasted apricot kernels (skin and tip removed), ground together into a powder, mix with one tael of melted yellow wax to form pills the size of bullets, chew them down with salt water. Some suggest hewing with fine yellow wax is good, sending down with tea is also effective. Yam, poria, and apricot kernels all nourish the Yang; particularly, yam greatly supplements the Yin, while apricot kernels help with airflow, thus balancing nourishment with passage. For those with dry throat and little energy, chew down Dongdong, ginseng in five-flavor soup.[103p]

Calamus San
Ingredients: 1 liang of stone calamus (1.9 inches segments); 5 liang of fresh Atractylodes. Grind the Atractylodes into pieces and immerse in rice wash for 7 days. Remove the Atractylodes and steam the calamus for about three zhong. Dry and grind into a fine powder. Take 2 qian each time with glutinous rice drink, three times a day. Alternatively, take the steamed pieces (about the size of a finger), place in the mouth after meals, chew occasionally, and swallow the saliva.[104p]

Tongshen Powder — Treatment for Deafness.
One whole scorpion, two earthworms, two dirt dogs, a small amount of musk, half a life of alum (half calcined), and five qian of realgar. Grind these into a fine powder. Each time, take a small amount, dip it in green onion white, and insert it into the ear. Hold your breath and sit facing the wall for a while, once every three days.

Ear Treatment Method
A piece of magnetite, size of a bean; the burnt powdered pangolin shell. Use these two ingredients wrapped in new cotton and stuff them in the affected ear. Hold a small piece of raw iron in your mouth. When you feel a sensation in the ear like wind and rain, you will be cured.

Chasing Wind Powder — Treatment for Deafness.
Equal parts of: rhizoma rhi, realgar, chuanxiong, acorus tatarinowii, whole scorpions, angelica dahurica, pogostemon cablin leaves, lamb's ear, mint, and bitter cloves. A little musk added. Grind these into a fine powder and blow a small amount into the nose. If lamb's ear is unavailable, add a little bit of brain matter.

Castor Oil Pill — Treatment for Deafness.
Remove the shell from castor beans, and mix with resin, yellow wax, peeled and fried almonds (double kernels) — each five qian. Add two and a half qian each of frankincense and salt-fried chuan beancurd. Grind these into a paste, roll into the size of jujube seeds, coat them with thin yellow wax, and poke two or three holes with a large needle. Use the ends to plug the ears; if yellowish liquid flows out overnight, you will be cured.

Ear Tube — Treatment for the Same Symptoms.
One qian each of pepperwort, chuan beancurd, acorus tatarinowii, and resin. Grind these into a powder and make a thin roll as a tube to insert into the ear. Change it once a day.[105p]

Xiong Huang San
Used for the same symptoms as above.
Xiong Huang, Fang Feng, Lian Shi, Shi Chang Pu, Wu Tou, and Chuan Jiao, each 2.5 qian; 10 big jujube pits. Grind the above into powder, place in a fragrant burner with a ball of mugwort the size of a small egg, then add half a qian of Huang Bo powder on top of the mugwort, and again add 2 qian of herbs on top of the mugwort, ignite them, and inhale the smoke from a tube.

Ear Deafness Formula
A bean and three cat’s whiskers not yielding oil, a small amount of musk mixed with true repair, refine honey into pills the size of wheat grains, wrap in cotton and toss into the ear.

Carp Gallbladder Ointment
Used for the same symptoms as above.
One carp gallbladder, a small amount of black donkey fat, and half a liang of raw oil. Mix well, place into a scallion tube for seven days, then drip into the ear.

Scorpion Tail Ointment
Used for the same symptoms as above.
Seven scorpion tails, roasted; 21 pieces of fermented black soybeans, choosing the larger ones and roasting them dry; seven purgative beans, removing the heart but not the oil. First grind the scorpion tails and black soybeans finely, separately grind the purgative beans into a paste, then mix them together. Mold into the size of a small jujube pit, use the small end of a scallion to create a hole, place one particle of the medicine inside, wrap securely with thin cotton. Place it in the ear overnight; if not effective, repeat until it's cleared.

Mouse Gallbladder Pills
Used for the same symptoms as above.
One qian of Zeng Qing, five fen of dragon brain, three qian of Ling Xiao flower, ground into fine powder. Each time, blow one character into the ear, then drop mouse gallbladder juice inside, sealing it with cotton until dawn.[106p]

Ricinus Seed Pill - Treats Long-lasting Deafness.

Twenty-one ricinus seeds, remove oil by stewing with soap pod, take half a block of fresh cooked raw ground dragon, two whole scorpions, roasted; with the heart of远志 removed, fire calcined magnetite, vinegar quenched seven times, grind finely, mix with two qian each of frankincense; make into fine powder, blend with yellow wax to form pills, stuff into the ears.

Long-lasting Deafness Recipe

Two and a half qian of Tianxiong, one piece of Aconite. Grind these into fine powder, take one chicken egg, open a hole, remove the yolk, add the medicine back into the shell, seal it up, have the chicken brood over it, and once the chick emerges, take it out, wrap in cotton and stuff into the ears for healing.

Deafness Chicken Egg Recipe

One fresh chicken egg, one seed of wild castor bean, remove the heart and membrane. First open a hole in the chicken egg, place the castor bean inside, seal with two layers of paper, return to the hen for brooding. Once the remaining chicks emerge, take the juice and drop it into the ears twice a day.

Ear Unblocking Pill - Treats Deafness.

One and a half liang each of benzoin, mulberry bark, and ferula gum; five fen of vermilion. Use seven wild castor beans, seven ricinus seeds, and seven garlic cloves, grind to a pulp, mix with the powdered medicine, form into pieces the size of jujube pits, and stuff into the ears.

Air Unblocking Powder - Treats Deafness.

Five qian each of pangolin and mole cricket, one qian of musk; grind these into fine powder, mix with scallion juice and stuff into the ears. Alternatively, grind it finely and place a small amount in a scallion tube to insert into the ears.[107p]

Formula for Deafness

  • 2.5 dimes of mercury, a single earthworm. Take one stalk of scallion from the cluster, remove the tip, place it in the mercury with the earthworm inside, then secure the head to prevent spillage. Wait for the worm to dissolve into water, then drip it into the ear.

Shengjin Toukuaisan

  • Good for treating previous symptoms.
  • One piece of Aconitum, two dimes of Asarum, 0.5 dimes of bile alum, one mouse gall. Grind together into a fine powder, mix with mouse gall, re-roast to dry, grind finely with musk (half a character), and blow into the ear using a goose feather tube. During blowing, hold clear tea in your mouth and wait for a moment.

Puhuang Ointment

  • Treats sudden deafness.
  • One dime each of Asarum and Puhuang, soak in apricot kernel broth, remove skins and double kernels; three dimes of dried malt. Grind into a fine powder, mix with apricots until like a paste, shape into size of a jujube seed, then stuff in the ear, changing daily.

Dragon Brain Ointment

  • 1.2 dimes of dragon brain, ground; 5 dimes of pepper seeds; 2.5 dimes of apricot kernels. Mash and mix evenly, wrap in cotton, size of a jujube seed, stuff in the ear, changing twice daily.

  • Treats conditions such as excessive heat accumulation, blocked ears, tinnitus, and ear sores.

Grind into powder, make into rice paste pills the size of tung seeds, and take 70-80 pills with rice soup.[108p]

Dragon Tooth Powder - Treats kidney deficiency heat toxins. Attacks from weakness can cause a constant ringing in the ears, similar to the sound of cicadas, and one should not rely solely on tonics. Ingredients: Dragon Tooth, Ginseng, White Poria, Ophiopogon, and Polygala, each ½ tael; Cinnabar, Iron Powder, Borneol, Cow Bile, and Musk, each 2.5 qian. Grind into a fine powder, mix well. Take ½ qian with boiling broth after meals, three times a day.

Grind into a fine powder and form pills the size of a tongzi. Take 40 pills before meals with a decoction of green onions and salt.

Chuanxiong and Angelica Drink - Treats the same condition. Ingredients: Chuanxiong, Angelica, and Chuanxiong, each 5 qian; Stone Calamus, Cinnamon, and White Peony, each 3 qian. Take 3 qian with 2 bowls of water, adding Perilla, Ginger, and Jujube, simmer until reduced to 1 bowl, strain. Consume at any time; if very cold, adjust by adding fresh Aconite.

Bupleurum Hearing Clarity Decoction - Treats ringing in the ears leading to deafness. Ingredients: Bupleurum 3 qian, Forsythia 4 qian, Hirudo (leech) 5 fen, stir-fried and ground; 3 Cicadas, wings and legs removed, ground; a small amount of Musk, ground; Angelica, Ginseng, and roasted Licorice, each 1 qian. Except for those requiring separate grinding, combine with 2 bowls of water, adding 3 slices of Ginger, simmer until reduced to 1 bowl, slightly warm, add leech powder, and simmer for one or two boils before eating, taken warm.[109p]

She Xiang San - Treats internal phantom sounds in the ear.

Jie Re Yin Zi: Treats Qi deficiency heat stagnation, causing deafness and pain in the ear with pus and blood discharge. Shu Nian Zi Tang: Treats ear pain with sores. Bai Long San: Treats children with kidney heat excess causing heat to rise to the ears, leading to the stagnation of fluids and the formation of pus. This can occur from water entering the ear during bathing, leading to dampness that congests blood and Qi, resulting in ear pus, known as "Teng Ear." If left untreated, it can lead to deafness. Ingredients: Alum (5 qian), Yellow Lead (5 qian), Dragon Bone (5 qian), and Musk (1 qian). Grind to a fine powder. First, use a cotton swab to clear the pus and water from the ear, then use the powder mixed with two ears twice a day, ensuring no wind enters.

Almonds, regardless of the quantity, should be roasted until they are reddish-black, then ground into a paste and wrapped in thin cotton. Place it inside the ear and change it three to four times a day. It is also effective to use it for scattered hair.

Aspirin of sweet flag treats ear pain.

One tael of sweet flag, with five qian of prepared aconite (removing skin and navel), mixed into a fine powder. Use an appropriate amount, mixed with oil, and drop into the ear. Another method is to make a vinegar ball the size of an almond, wrapped in cotton and placed in the ear, changed three times a day. Another method is to crush sweet flag and inject the natural juice into the ear; it is highly effective.

Tongqi San treats ear blockage.

Ingredients include: peeled Prunus mume kernels, five qian of peony, ginseng, one tael of rhubarb, yam, and the peeled parts of cassia, three areca nuts, peony bark, aromatic wood, and fine xinyi (all two qian and five fen). Grind them together into a fine powder. Each dose is one qian, taken with warm wine on an empty stomach.

Mantongzi San treats internal heat and ear pus discharge.

Ingredients: mantongzi, red peony, raw rhubarb, mulberry bark, chamomile flowers, red poria, chuan shengma, and lily bulbs (de-heart), houttuynia, qianhu, and roasted licorice (all one qian). Songhua San treats the symptoms mentioned above.

Ingredients: five qian of burnt alum, two and a half qian each of hemp flower, aromatic wood, pine resin, and rouge. Grind and sift them finely. First, cleanse the ear with a cotton stick, then blow the medicine into the ear.[112p]

　　枯矾　鰞鲗骨　黄连去须　龙骨各一两　右为细末，以绵裹枣核大，塞耳中，日三易。
　　麝香散　治前证。
　　桑螵蛸一个，炙　麝香一字　右为末，研令匀，每用半字掺耳。如有脓，先用绵杖子捻干。一法用麝香少，黄丹多，研匀入耳。
　　禹余粮丸　治前证。
　　禹余粮火烧酢淬，七次　鰞鲗鱼骨　釜底墨　伏龙肝各二钱五分　生附子　右件为末，以绵裹如皂角子大，塞耳，日再易之。如不瘥者，内有虫也。
　　葱涎膏　治耵聍塞耳，聋，不可强挑。　　葱汁三合　细辛去苗　附子炮，去皮，各二钱　右以细辛、附子为末，葱汁调如枣核大，塞耳中。
　　耳聤方
　　龙骨　枯矾　胭脂　海螵蛸各等分　麝香少许　右为细末，先缴耳净，将药干吹。
　　菖蒲散　治前证。
　　菖蒲焙　狼毒　磁石火煅，酢淬　附子炮，去皮　枯矾各五钱　右为细末，以羊髓和少许，绵裹塞耳中。[113p]

Bailian Powder - For treating pre-corporeal symptoms.
Dry Alum, Fish Bone, Coptis Chinensis (with roots removed), Dragon Bone, each one tael. Grind to a fine powder, wrap it in cotton the size of a jujube pit, and plug it in the ear, changing it three times a day.

Musk Powder - For treating pre-corporeal symptoms.
One dried silkworm, roasted; a small amount of musk. Grind these to a powder, mix evenly, and use half a character to sprinkle in the ear. If there is pus, first use a cotton swab to dry it. Alternatively, use a bit less musk and more yellow lead, grind evenly, and place in the ear.

Yu Yuliang Pill - For treating pre-corporeal symptoms.
Yu Yuliang is calcined with vinegar, seven times. Fish bones, black soot from a cauldron, and liver of a hidden dragon, each two and a half qian. Raw Aconite. Grind these items into a powder and wrap in cotton the size of a soap pod, plug it in the ear, changing it twice a day. If it does not heal, it indicates the presence of worms inside.

Scallion Salve - For treating earwax blockage and deafness; do not forcibly extract.
Three portions of scallion juice, fine chives (roots removed), roasted Aconite (peel removed), each two qian. Grind the fine chives and Aconite into a powder, mix with scallion juice to the size of a jujube pit, and plug it in the ear.

Ear Tingling Formula
Dragon bone, dry alum, rouge, and sea silkworm, each in equal parts, with a small amount of musk. Grind these to a fine powder, first clean the ear, then dry the medicine, and blow it in.

Acorus Powder - For treating pre-corporeal symptoms.
Dried Acorus, Wolf Poison, magnetite tempered with fire and vinegar, roasted Aconite (peel removed), and dry alum, each five qian. Grind these to a fine powder, mix with a bit of sheep marrow, and wrap it to plug in the ear.[113p]

　　竹蛀散　治前证。
　　苦竹蛀末　枯矾各二钱　胭脂五分　麝香一钱　右研极细，以绵杖子拭之，用鹅毛管吹一字入耳。
　　蝎倍散　治前证。
　　全蝎烧存性，三钱　五倍子炒，一两　枯矾一钱　麝香少许　右为细末，研匀，每用少许吹耳中。一方加干胭脂。
　　立效散　治前证。
　　陈橘皮灯上烧黑，一钱，为末　麝香少许右研匀，每用少许，先以绵拭耳内，脓净吹之。
　　香附散　治前证。
　　香附去毛，研为末　右以绵杖送入耳。
　　附子丸　治耳聋出脓，疼痛及耵聍塞耳。　　附子炮，去皮脐　菖蒲米泔，浸焙　蓖麻仁另研　枯白矾　松脂各一两研　干胭脂半两　杏仁二两，去皮尖双仁，炒，另研　右为细末，研匀，镕黄蜡和捻如枣核大，针穿一孔，令透，塞耳中，日一换。或治聤聍，不用黄蜡，只捣成膏，绵裹如枣核大，塞耳。[114p]

Bamboo Weevil Powder: For treating ear symptoms.
Bitter bamboo weevil powder, dried alum each 2 qian, rouge 5 fen, musk 1 qian. Grind them very finely, use a cotton stick to apply it, and blow a small amount into the ear with a goose feather tube.

Scorpion Powder: For treating ear symptoms.
Whole scorpions, roasted to retain their essence, 3 qian; five taxa, stir-fried, 1 liang; dried alum 1 qian; a small amount of musk. Grind these into a fine powder and mix evenly, using a small amount to blow into the ear. One formula adds dried rouge.

Immediate Effect Powder: For treating ear symptoms.
Aged tangerine peel, burned black over a lamp, 1 qian, ground into powder; a small amount of musk. Grind these together evenly, using a small amount first to wipe the inside of the ear, then blow it out clean.

Atractylodes Powder: For treating ear symptoms.
Atractylodes without hairs, ground into powder. Use this along with a cotton stick to apply it into the ear.

Aconite Pills: For treating deafness with pus, pain, and earwax blockage.
Roasted aconite, peeled and cored; calamus grains soaked and roasted; castor seeds ground separately; dried white alum, pine resin each 1 liang, ground; dried rouge half a liang; almond 2 liang, peeled and double-kernel removed, stir-fried and ground separately. Combine into a fine powder, mix evenly, melt with yellow wax, form into the size of a jujube seed, pierce with a needle to make it breathable, and insert into the ear, changing daily. Alternatively, for earwax blockage, do not use yellow wax, just pound into a paste, wrap in cotton to the size of a jujube seed, and insert into the ear.[114p]

　　耳脓方
　　密陀僧一钱　轻粉五分　麝香一字　右为细末，先以绵拭耳内，脓却掺药。
　　三黄散　治耳内流脓。
　　雄黄　硫黄　雌黄各等分　右为细末，以少许吹入耳中。
　　二圣散　治耳内出脓水。
　　羌活　白附子炮，各一两　右为细末，用猪、羊肾各一只，切开，每只入药末五分，不得着盐，湿纸裹煨熟，五更初，温酒嚼下，续吃粥压之。
　　无忧散　治前证。
　　黄芪　木通　桑白皮　陈皮各一两　胡椒　白朮　木香各五钱　牵牛头末，四两　右俱为细末，每服三五钱，食后以姜汁调下。
　　曾青散　治耳内疮。
　　雄黄七钱五分　曾青五钱　黄芩二钱五分　右为细末，研匀，每用少许纳耳中，有脓汁，用绵杖子拭干用之。
　　黄连散　治前证。
　　黄连五钱　枯白矾七钱五分　右为细末，每用少许，绵裹，纳耳中。[115p]

Ear Pus Formulas

Mi Tuo Seng Powder
1 qian of Mi Tuo Seng, 5 fen of light powder, 1 character of musk. Grind finely and first use cotton to wipe the inside of the ear, then mix in the medicine with the pus.

San Huang Powder
For treating pus inside the ear. Equal parts of realgar, sulfur, and orpiment, ground finely. Blow a small amount into the ear.

Er Sheng Powder
For treating pus and water discharge from the ear. 1 liang each of Qiang Huo and Bai Fu Zi (prepared), ground finely. Using one pig and one sheep kidney, cut open and put 5 fen of the medicine into each; do not let it touch salt. Wrap in damp paper and steam until cooked. At dawn, chew with warm wine and continue to eat porridge with it.

Wu You Powder
For treating previous symptoms. 1 liang each of Huang Qi, Mu Tong, Sang Bai Pi, and Chen Pi; 5 qian each of pepper, Bai Zhu, and Mu Xiang; 4 liang of Qian Niu Tou powder, all ground finely. Take 3-5 qian after meals mixed with ginger juice.

Zeng Qing Powder
For treating sores inside the ear. 7.5 qian of realgar, 5 qian of Zeng Qing, and 2.5 qian of Huang Qin, ground finely and mixed. Use a small amount to insert into the ear. If there's pus, clean it with a cotton stick.

Huang Lian Powder
For treating previous symptoms. 5 qian of Huang Lian and 7.5 qian of dried white alum, ground finely. Use a small amount wrapped in cotton and insert into the ear.[115p]

　　柴胡栀子散　治三焦及足少阳经风热，耳内作痒，生疮或出水疼痛，或胸乳间作痛，或寒热往来。　　柴胡　栀子炒　牡丹皮各一钱　茯苓　芍药　当归　牛蒡子炒，各七分　甘草五分　右，水煎服。一名栀子清肝散。
　　当归川芎散　治手足少阳经血虚疮证；或风热耳内痒痛，生疮出水；或头目不清，寒热少食；或妇女经水不调，胸膈不利，腹胁痞痛。　　当归　川芎　柴胡　白朮　白芍药各一钱　山栀炒，一钱二分　牡丹皮　白茯苓各八分　蔓荆子　甘草各五分　右水煎服。若肝气不平，寒热，加地骨皮。肝气实，加柴胡、黄芩。气血虚，加参、芪、归、地。脾虚，饮食少思，加苓、朮。脾虚，胸膈不利，加参、芪。痰滞，胸膈不利，加朮、半。肝气不顺，胸膈不利，或小腹痞满攻痛，加青皮。肝血虚，胸膈不利，或小腹痞满，时作痛，加熟地。肝血虚寒，小腹时痛，加肉桂。日晡发热，加归、地。[116p]

Chai Hu Zhi Zi San treats wind-heat in the three jiaos and the foot Shaoyang channel, presenting symptoms like itching in the ears, sores or discharge with pain, chest or breast pain, or alternating chills and fever. The ingredients include: Chai Hu, Zhi Zi (stir-fried), Mu Dan Pi, each 1 qian; Fu Ling, Shao Yao, Dang Gui, Niu Bang Zi (stir-fried), each 7 fen; and Gan Cao 5 fen. These are simmered in water for administration. It is also known as Zhi Zi Qing Gan San.

Dang Gui Chuan Xiong San treats blood deficiency sores in the hand and foot Shaoyang channels; symptoms may include itching and pain in the ears due to wind-heat, sores and discharge; or unclear head and eyes, chills and fever, reduced appetite; or irregular menstruation in women, insufficient chest and diaphragmatic function, and abdominal or flank distension and pain. The ingredients include: Dang Gui, Chuan Xiong, Chai Hu, Bai Zhu, Bai Shao, each 1 qian; Shan Zhi (stir-fried), 1 qian 2 fen; Mu Dan Pi and Bai Fu Ling, each 8 fen; Man Jing Zi and Gan Cao, each 5 fen. These are simmered in water for administration. If liver Qi is unbalanced, add Di Gu Pi. For excessive liver Qi, add Chai Hu and Huang Qin. If Qi and blood are deficient, add Ren Shen, Huang Qi, Dang Gui, and Di Huang. For spleen deficiency, with reduced appetite, add Ling and Zhu. If there is spleen deficiency with insufficient chest and diaphragmatic function, add Ren Shen and Huang Qi. For phlegm stagnation resulting in chest and diaphragmatic blockage, add Zhu and Ban. If liver Qi is not smooth causing chest and diaphragmatic obstruction, or if there is distension and pain in the lower abdomen, add Qing Pi. For liver blood deficiency causing chest and diaphragmatic obstruction, or distension and pain in the lower abdomen occurring intermittently, add Shu Di. For cold due to liver blood deficiency with pain in the lower abdomen, add Rou Gui. If there is fever in the late afternoon, add Dang Gui and Di Huang.[116p]

　　加味地黄丸　治肝肾阴虚疮证，或耳内痒痛出水；或眼昏痰气喘嗽，或作渴发热，小便赤濇等证。　　干山药　山茱萸肉　牡丹皮　泽泻　白茯苓　熟地黄　生地黄　柴胡　五味子各另为末，等分　右，将二地黄掏碎，酒拌湿杵膏，入前末和匀，加炼蜜为丸，如桐子大，每服百丸，空心白汤下。不应，用加减八味丸。
　　立验散　治蜒蚰入耳。
　　川芎　白芷　夜明沙炒　猪牙皂角炙　南星炮，各七钱五分　百部　白丁香　藜芦各四钱　草乌五钱　砒霜另研　荜茇各二钱　海金沙二钱五分　右为细末，研匀，临时更用铅丹调色匀，磁器收。如蜒蚰入耳，取少许酢调，以细翎蘸药入耳，微吹，令药气行，立出。药不得多，多即蜒蚰成水不出。如蝎螫，先点少酢在螫处，掺药半字许，擦令热即效。[117p]

Jiawei Dihuang Pill treats liver and kidney yin deficiency causing sores, or itchiness and pain in the ear with discharge; or blurriness in the eyes, phlegm, breathlessness, or thirst with fever, and red, painful urination. The ingredients are: dried yam, cornelian cherry fruit, peony root, swamp plantain, white poria, cooked rehmannia, raw rehmannia, bupleurum, and schisandra, each ground into powder in equal amounts. Then, crush the two types of rehmannia, mix with wine to make a paste, combine with the powders, and add honey to form pills the size of a Chinese chestnut. Take one hundred pills with warm water on an empty stomach. If there are side effects, use the modified Eight Flavor Pill.

Liyansan treats insects entering the ear. The ingredients are: Sichuan lovage, white angelica, night-shining sand (stir-fried), pig's tooth soapberry (roasted), and southern star (prepared), each 7.5 grams; hundred parts, white clove, and rhizoma phragmitis, each 4 grams; black cocoon 5 grams; arsenic prepared separately; and pipul, each 2 grams; sea gold silk 2.5 grams. Grind all into a fine powder, mix thoroughly, and if needed, adjust color with lead cinnabar in a porcelain container.

If an insect enters the ear, take a small amount of vinegar to mix, dip a fine feather in the medicine, place it in the ear, and blow lightly to allow the medicinal vapor to circulate, prompting immediate expulsion. Do not use too much medicine, as too much will turn the insect into liquid and not come out. For scorpion stings, first apply a small amount of vinegar to the sting site and then sprinkle some medicine to rub in until warm, which will have an immediate effect.[117p]

　　加减龙荟丸 【《医鉴》，下同】 　治痰火上升耳鸣。　　麝香五分　草龙胆酒洗　当归酒洗　栀子炒　黄芩　青皮各一两　木香二钱半　大黄酒蒸　青黛　柴胡各五钱　芦荟　牛胆南星各三钱　右为末，神曲糊和丸，菉豆大，姜汤下二十丸，日三服，七日后用针砂酒，以通其气。一本无牛胆。
　　针砂酒　治证见上。
　　针砂一两　穿山甲末一钱　右，以穿山甲拌针砂，养一昼夜，拣出山甲，将针砂以酒一碗浸三四日，噙酒口内，外用磁石一块绵裹，塞耳。忌怒。
　　通明利气汤　治虚火痰气郁于耳中，或闭或鸣，痰火炽盛，痞满烦躁。　　贝母一钱五分　陈皮一钱二分五厘　黄连　黄芩并酒浸，又用猪胆汁拌炒，七分五厘　黄蘗酒炒　栀子炒　元参酒洗，各一钱　苍朮盐水炒　白朮　香附童便炒　生干地黄姜汁炒　槟榔各五分　川芎四分　木香二分五厘　甘草二分　右銼，作一贴，入姜三片，水煎，入竹沥五匙服。[118p]

Jia Jian Long Hui Wan
Treats phlegm and fire rising, causing tinnitus.

  • 0.5 grams of musk
  • 1 tael each of herbal dragon gall, angelica root (washed with wine), fried gardenia fruit, and yellow qin
  • 2.5 qian of wood fragrance
  • 0.5 tael each of rhubarb (steamed with wine), green indigo, and bupleurum
  • 0.3 tael each of aloe vera and southern stargrass
    Grind the above into powder, mix with fermented sorghum dough to form pills the size of a mung bean. Take twenty pills with ginger soup three times a day. After seven days, use needle sand wine to facilitate the movement of qi. One version does not include southern stargrass.

Needle Sand Wine
Treats the conditions mentioned above.

  • 1 tael of needle sand
  • 0.1 tael of ground pangolin
    Mix the pangolin with needle sand, let it rest for one day and night, then remove the pangolin. Soak the needle sand in a bowl of wine for three to four days, hold the wine in the mouth, and externally use a piece of magnet wrapped in cotton to block the ear. Avoid anger.

Tong Ming Li Qi Decoction
Treats deficiency fire and phlegm-qi accumulation in the ear, which may be blocked or ringing, with excessive phlegm fire causing fullness and restlessness.

  • 1.5 qian of fritillaria
  • 1.25 qian of aged tangerine peel
  • Yellow liand and yellow qin, soak in wine, then mix with fried pig bile juice, 0.75 qian
  • Fried berberine wine
  • Fried gardenia
  • 1 qian of original ginseng washed with wine
  • 0.5 qian each of saltwater fried atractylodes, white atractylodes, and sweet gale fried with urine
  • 0.5 qian each of raw dry rehmannia and ginger juice fried
  • 0.25 qian of betel nut
  • 0.4 qian of chuanxiong
  • 0.25 qian of wood fragrance
  • 0.2 qian of licorice
    Grind the above ingredients, prepare one dose, add three slices of ginger, and decoct in water. Add five spoonfuls of bamboo juice before taking.[118p]

　　复聪汤 【丹溪】 　治痰火上攻，耳鸣耳聋。　　半夏　赤茯苓　陈皮　甘草　萹蓄　木通　瞿麦　黄蘗盐炒，各一钱　右銼，作一贴，入姜三片，水煎。

　　滋肾通气汤 【《回春》，下同】 　治肾虚耳鸣欲聋。　　当归　川芎　白芍药　生干地黄酒炒，各一钱　知母　黄蘗　黄芩并酒炒　柴胡　白芷　香附炒，各七分　右銼，作一贴，空心，水煎温服。

Fu Cong Decoction [Danxi]
Treats phlegm fire surging upwards, causing tinnitus and deafness.
Ingredients: Banxia, red poria, aged tangerine peel, licorice, beebalm, mu tong, qu mai, and salt-fried Huangbo, each 3 grams. Grind together to make a paste, add three slices of ginger, and boil in water.

Da Bu Pill [From "Yi Jian"]
Treats tinnitus with a desire for deafness.
Ingredients: Eight taels of Huangbo, grated, mixed with human milk, dried, and then stir-fried in salt water until brown. Mash into a fine powder, form into water pills the size of a wax gourd, and take one hundred pills with hollow salt water. Also known as Du Sheng Wan.

Zi Shen Tong Qi Decoction [From "Hui Chun", same below]
Treats kidney deficiency with tinnitus and a desire for deafness.
Ingredients: Dang gui, chuan xiong, white peony, and raw rehmannia stir-fried with wine, each 3 grams; zhi mu, Huangbo, and Huangqin stir-fried with wine, along with chai hu, bai zhi, and xiang fu stir-fried, each 4.5 grams; grind together to make a paste, take on an empty stomach, and boil in water for warm consumption.

Long Dan Decoction
Treats anger stirring gallbladder fire, causing left ear deafness.
Ingredients: Huanglian and Huangqin stir-fried, zhizi stir-fried, dang gui, aged tangerine peel, niu dan, and south star anise, each 3 grams; long dan and xiang fu, each 2.5 grams; yuanshen 1.5 grams; qing dai and mu xiang, each 1.5 grams; dry ginger stir-fried black, 1 gram. Grind together to make a paste, add three slices of ginger, boil in water, and add 1.5 grams of Yuan Ming powder before consumption.[119p]

　　滋阴地黄汤　治色欲动相火，致右耳聋。　　熟地黄一钱五分　山药　山茱萸肉　白芍药　当归　川芎各八两　牡丹皮　泽泻　白茯苓　石菖蒲　远志　知母盐酒炒　黄蘗盐酒炒，各六分　右銼，作一贴，水煎服，空心。亦治大病后耳聋。
　　清聪化痰丸　治饮食厚味，挟怒气以动肝胃之火，致耳聋耳鸣，壅闭不闻声音。　　橘红去白，盐水洗　赤茯苓　蔓荆子各一两　片芩酒炒，八钱　黄连酒炒　白芍药酒浸，煨　生地黄酒洗　柴胡　半夏姜制，各七钱　人参六钱　青皮酢炒，五钱　生甘草四钱　右为末，葱汤浸，蒸饼和丸，菉豆大，茶清下百丸。
　　黄龙散　治沐浴水入耳中成脓耳。亦治小儿聤耳。　　枯白矾　龙骨煅黄丹水飞　干胭脂烧灰　海螵蛸煅，一钱　麝香少许　右为末，先以纸捻拭干脓水，乃以绵捻蘸药入耳，日日易之。[120p]

Zi Yin Di Huang Decoction: Treats sexual desire-driven fire, leading to deafness in the right ear. Ingredients: 1.5 qian of熟地黄, 8 liang each of 山药, 山茱萸肉, 白芍药, 当归, 川芎, and 6 fen each of 牡丹皮, 泽泻, 白茯苓, 石菖蒲, 遠志, 知母 (salt wine roasted), and 黄蘗 (salt wine roasted). Grind together to make a decoction and take on an empty stomach. Also treats deafness after major illness.

Qing Cong Hua Tan Pill: Treats ear deafness and ringing caused by excessive eating and anger stirring liver and stomach fire, leading to blockage and inability to hear sounds. Ingredients: 1 liang of橘红 (white part removed and washed in salt water), 赤茯苓, and 蔓荆子, 8 qian of片芩 (roasted in wine), roasted 黄连, and white peony soaked in wine, 7 qian each of生地黄 (washed in wine), 柴胡, and 半夏 (prepared with ginger), 6 qian of 人参, 5 qian of 青皮 (fried in vinegar), and 4 qian of 生甘草. Grind into powder, soak in scallion broth, steam into pills the size of mung beans, and take with clear tea, 100 pills.

Huang Long Powder: Treats ear inflammation from bathing water entering the ear. Also for children's ear deafness. Ingredients: 凋白矾, dragon bone roasted, yellow ochre water, dried lipstick burned to ash, and dried sea pig shell roasted, 1 qian; a little musk. Grind together, first use paper to wipe away pus and water, then dip cotton in the medicine and place in the ear, changing daily.[120p]

　　补骨脂丸 【《入门》】 　治劳损耳聋。　　磁石煅酢淬，一两二钱五分　熟地黄　当归身　川芎　肉桂　菟丝子　川椒　破故纸　杜仲　白蒺藜　胡卢巴　白芷　菖蒲各二钱　右为末，蜜丸，梧手大，空心葱白汤下五十丸。
　　聪耳汤 【《医鉴》】 　治耳重听不清。　　黄蘗酒炒，一钱　当归身酒洗　白芍药酒炒　生地黄酒洗　川芎　知母酒炒　陈皮　乌药　白芷　防风　羌活酒洗独活酒洗　薄荷　蔓荆子　槁本酒洗，各一钱　细辛七分　右銼，作一贴，水煎，食后服。服后低头睡一时。
　　地黄汤 【《本草》】 　治肾经热，右耳听事不真，每心中着意，则转觉重虚而鸣疼痛。　　磁石煅淬为末，二两　生干地黄酒洗，一两五钱　甘草五钱　枳壳　羌活　桑皮　防风　黄芩　木通各一两　右为粗末，每四钱，水煎，日二服。[121p]

Treats fatigue and deafness.

Prepared rehmannia, 2 qian;

Bai zhi, 2 qian;
Acorus, 2 qian.
Grind the above into a powder, form into honey pills, the size of a Wutou, take 50 pills with scallion white broth.

Cong Er Tang (From "Yijian")
Treats heavy and unclear hearing.
Huangbo, stir-fried with wine, 1 qian;
Angelica, washed with wine;
White peony, stir-fried with wine;
Raw rehmannia, washed with wine;
Chuanxiong;
Zhi mu, stir-fried with wine;
Chen pi;

Bai zhi;
Fang feng;

Mint;
Viburnum fruit;
Dried herbs, washed with wine, each 1 qian;
Xi xin, 7 fen.
Grind the above, make into a paste, decoct in water, take after meals. After taking, sleep with head lowered for one hour.

Di Huang Tang (From "Bencao")
Treats heat in the kidney channel, right ear hears unclear; whenever the mind focuses, it feels heavy, empty, and painful.
Calcinated magnetite, 2 taels;
Raw dry rehmannia, washed with wine, 1.5 taels;
Licorice, 5 qian;
Zhi ke;
Qiang huo;
Mulberry bark;
Fang feng;
Huangqin;
Mugwort, each 1 tael.
Grind the above into a coarse powder, take 4 qian, decoct in water, take twice daily.[121p]

　　荆芥连翘汤 【《回春》】 　治两耳肿痛，由肾经有风热。　　荆芥穗　连翘　防风　当归　川芎　白芍药　柴胡　枳壳　黄芩　栀子炒　白芷　桔梗各七分　甘草五分　右銼，作一贴，水煎，食后温服。
　　红绵散 【丹溪】 　治脓耳。
　　枯矾　海螵蛸各一钱　干胭脂五分　麝香一字　右研匀，先以绵捻子拭去耳脓水，尽却，以纸捻蘸药掺入耳中，即干。一方无海螵蛸。
　　抵圣散 【东垣】 　治耳中脓出，经年不愈。　　鰞鲗骨三钱　乳香二钱　枯白矾　干胭脂　轻粉各一钱　麝香五分　右细末，或掺入，或吹入耳中。
　　明矾散 【丹溪】 　治肾经热上冲于耳，使津液凝滞为稠脓清汁，或沐浴水入耳停滞为脓，但不疼。若不差，变成脓。　　枯白矾　龙骨各三钱　黄丹二钱　麝香少许　干胭脂一钱　右为末，先去脓水，次吹药入。[122p]

Jingjie Lianqiao Decoction (from "Huichun")
For the treatment of swelling and pain in both ears caused by wind-heat in the kidney channel.
Ingredients: seven parts of Jingjie spikes, Lianqiao, Fangfeng, Danggui, Chuanxiong, Baishao, Chaihu, Zhike, Huangqin, and Zizhi, each seven parts; five parts of Gancao. Grind together, prepare into a paste, boil in water, and take warm after meals.

Hongmian Powder (from Danxi)
For the treatment of ear suppuration.
Ingredients: one qian each of dried alum and Haipiaoxiao; five fen of dried rouge; a character's worth of musk. Grind evenly, first use cotton to wipe away the ear pus completely, then use a paper twist to dip in the medicine and insert it into the ear. It should be dry. One recipe does not require Haipiaoxiao.

Disheng Powder (from Dongyuan)
For the treatment of ear pus persisting for years.
Ingredients: three qian of fish bone, two qian of frankincense, one qian each of dried white alum, dried rouge, and light powder; five fen of musk. Grind to a fine powder and either mix it in or blow it into the ear.

Mingfan Powder (from Danxi)
For the treatment of heat in the kidney channel rising to the ear, causing fluid to congeal into thick pus or water stagnating in the ear, leading to pus but no pain. If untreated, it may turn into pus.
Ingredients: three qian each of dried white alum and dragon bone; two qian of yellow lead; a small amount of musk; one qian of dried rouge. First remove the pus water, then blow in the powder.[122p]

　　吹耳散 【《回春》】 　治肾经风热，耳内出脓汁。　　干胭脂　海螵蛸　枯白矾　龙骨　赤石脂　密陀僧煅　胆矾　青黛　硼砂　黄连各一钱　龙脑二分　麝香一分右为细末，先去脓水，次吹药入。
　　元参贝母场 【《医鉴》】 　治耳热出汁作痒，乃痰也，肾火上炎也。　　防风　贝母　天花粉　黄蘗盐水炒　白茯苓　元参　白芷　蔓荆子　天麻　半夏制，各一钱　甘草五分　右銼，作一贴，入姜三片，水煎，食后服。

　　柴胡清肝散　治肝胆三焦风热疮疡，或怒火憎寒发热，或疮毒结于两耳前后，或身外侧至足，或两胸乳小腹下，或股内侧至足等证。　　柴胡　黄芩炒　人参各三分　山栀炒　川芎各五分　连翘　桔梗各四分　甘草三分　右，水煎服。

Used to treat kidney channel wind-heat, with pus-like discharge from the ear.

Yuan Shen Mother-of-Pearl Powder (from "Medical Reflection")
Used to treat ear heat with discharge and itching, indicating phlegm and kidney fire rising.
Ingredients:

  • Fangfeng

Used to treat qi obstruction and deafness.

  • Stone calamus one inch
  • One seed of croton

    Grind into powder, mix with onion saliva, shape into a jujube kernel size, and insert into the ear.

Chai Hu Clear Liver Powder
Used to treat wind-heat sores or ulcers in the liver, gallbladder, and triple burner, or when anger and aversion to cold cause fever, or when sores or toxins are located around both ears, or on the outer body down to the feet, or in the chest, lower abdomen, or inner thighs down to the feet.
Ingredients:

  • Chai hu
  • Stir-fried yellow qin
  • Ginseng three fen each;
  • Stir-fried gardenia and chuanxiong five fen each;
  • Forsythia and platycodon four fen each;
  • Licorice three fen.
    Decoct in water and take.

Musk Finger Citron Powder
Used to treat five types of ear bleeding.[123p]

　　麝香少许　人牙煅过存性，出火毒　右为细末，每用少许吹耳内，即干。及治小儿痘疮出现面靥者，酒调一字服之，即出。
　　水银膏　治月蚀疮在两耳上及窍旁，随月盈虚以为消长。　　水银二钱五分　胡粉研　松脂　黄连去须为末，各五钱　右，先熬猪脂令沸，下松脂诸末及水银，搅令匀，磁盒盛。先以盐汤洗净疮，涂敷，日三五度。
　　胡粉散　治月蚀疮。
　　胡粉炒微黄　白矾　虢丹煅　黄连净　轻粉各二钱　胭脂一钱　麝香少许　右为末，先以温浆水入盐洗拭，后掺药；如疮干，麻油调敷。
　　黄芪内托散　治耳肿痛。
　　川芎　当归　黄芪各二钱　白朮　金银花　天花粉　皂角针各一钱　甘草　泽泻各五分　右，水三锺，煎八分，食前服。
　　仙方活命饮　治前证。
　　穿山甲蛤粉炒黄　白芷　防风　赤芍　花粉　归尾　乳香　没药　川贝母　皂角刺　甘草各一钱　金银花　陈皮各三钱　酒一碗，煎数沸，温服。[124p]

A small amount of musk, human bone calcined to preserve its potency, is toxic when heated. Grind it into a fine powder, and use a small amount to blow into the ear until dry. For treating smallpox in children where facial marks appear, mix a character with wine and take it.

Mercury ointment treats moon-eclipsed sores located on both ears and around the openings, following the waxing and waning of the moon for healing. Use 2.5 taels of mercury, five taels each of ground hu powder, pine resin, and yellow lily, with the hairs removed. First, boil pig fat until boiling, then add the pine resin and other powders along with mercury, mixing evenly and storing in a ceramic container. First cleanse the sores with saltwater, then apply three to five times a day.

Hu powder powder treats moon-eclipsed sores.

Slightly roasted hu powder, white alum, calcined realgar, purified yellow lily, and light powder each 2 taels; one tael of rouge and a small amount of musk, ground into a powder. First, wash with warm rice water and salt, then blend with the medicine; if the sores are dry, apply with sesame oil.

Huangqi mixed internal powder treats swollen and painful ears.

Chuanxiong, angelica, and Huangqi each 2 taels; white attractor, honeysuckle, tianhuafen, and soap pod spines each 1 tael; licorice and poria cocos each 0.5 tael. Boil with three bowls of water until reduced to two bowls, and take before meals.

Xianfang Huoming Decoction treats the previous symptoms.

Roasted pangolin shell powder, white angelica, protective wind, red peony, flower pollen, angelica root, frankincense, myrrh, chuan bei mu, soap pod thorn, and licorice each 1 tael; honeysuckle and dried tangerine peel each 3 taels. Boil in a bowl of wine until boiling and take warm.[124p]

　　托里消毒散　治前证。
　　人参随证加减　黄芪盐水拌炒　当归　川芎　白芍药炒　白朮炒　白茯苓各一钱　金银花　白芷各七分　甘草　连翘各五分　右，水煎服。
　　参芪内托散　治前证。
　　人参　黄芪蜜炙　当归　川芎　厚朴姜炙　防风　桔梗炒　白芷　紫草　官桂　木香　甘草等分　右，入糯米一撮。水煎服。
　　十宣散　治前证。
　　人参　黄芪制　当归各二钱　川芎　甘草炙　桔梗　白芷　防风　厚朴各一钱　桂心三分　右为细末，每服一钱或二钱，木香汤下。
　　黄连消毒散　治前证。
　　黄连炒　羌活各一分　黄芩　黄蘗　桔梗　槁本　防己各五分　当归尾　连翘　防风　独活　知母炒　生地黄各四分　人参　甘草各三分　黄芪　苏木　陈皮　泽泻各二分　右(口父)咀，为粗末，煎服。[125p]

Tori Disinfection Powder - Treats the previous symptoms.
Add or subtract ginseng according to the symptoms, stir-fried astragalus with saltwater, one qian each of angelica, chuanxiong, fried white peony, fried white atractylodes, and fried white poria; seven fen each of honeysuckle and white vector; five fen each of licorice and forsythia. Decoction and take.

Ginseng and Astragalus Inner Disinfection Powder - Treats the previous symptoms.
Ginseng and honey-fried astragalus, angelica, chuanxiong, fried magnolia bark with ginger, fangfeng, fried platycodon, white vector, purple gromwell, cinnamon, amomum, and licorice in equal parts; add a pinch of glutinous rice. Decoction and take.

Ten Dissemination Powder - Treats the previous symptoms.
Ginseng, honey-prepared astragalus, and angelica, each two qian; chuanxiong, fried licorice, platycodon, white vector, fangfeng, and magnolia bark, each one qian; three fen of cinnamon. Grind into a fine powder; take one or two qian with wood incense decoction.

Coptis Disinfection Powder - Treats the previous symptoms.
Fried coptis and qinghao, each one fen; yellow sheng, huangbo, platycodon, dried root, and fangji, each five fen; four fen each of angelica tail, forsythia, fangfeng, duhuo, and fried anemarrhena; three fen each of ginseng and licorice; two fen each of astragalus, red sandalwood, dried orange peel, and water plantain. Grind into coarse powder and decoct for use.[125p]

　　远志酒　能托散诸毒。
　　远志不拘多少，用米泔浸洗，椎去心　右为末，每服三钱，用好酒一锺调，迟少顷，澄清饮之，以滓敷患处。
　　清肝流气饮 【《疮疡全书》，下同】 　治耳痔、耳蕈、耳痈、耳湿、耳烂。　　枳壳　桔梗　黄芩　小柴胡　青皮炒　前胡　羌活　薄荷　生地黄　乌药　甘草生　防风　川芎　白芷　石膏　赤芍　右(口父)咀，水煎服。
　　定痛降气汤　前证服流气饮后，即服此方。　　紫苏叶　厚朴　陈皮　甘草生　半夏　前胡　川芎　防风　白芍药　白芷　当归身　黄蘗　知母　乳香　柴胡　右，姜三片，枣一枚，煎服，不拘时。
　　炼石散　治耳旁石疽，坚如石块，其色不变。　　鹿角烧灰，八两　白蔹三两　粗厉黄石二斤　右，用好酢五升，先烧石通红，淬酢中，再烧再淬，酢尽方止，为末，加二味末，将剩下酢调如泥，涂上，消软。炙处亦涂之。
古今图书集成医部全录卷一百三十七

耳门
[126p]

Yuan Zhi Wine can dispel various toxins.
Yuan Zhi is not limited by quantity; soak and wash it with rice water, pound out the heart, and fine grind it into powder. Each dose is three qian, mixed with a cup of good wine. After a little while, let it settle, drink the clear liquid, and apply the sediment to the affected area.

Clear Liver Qi Drink
This treats ear hemorrhoids, ear fungi, ear carbuncles, ear dampness, and ear ulcers.
Ingredients: Bitter Orange Peel, Platycodon Root, Scutellaria, Minor Bupleurum, stir-fried Green Peel, Radix Notopterygii, Mint, Fresh Rehmannia Root, Wu Yao, Fresh Licorice, Fang Feng, Chuanxiong, White Atractylodes, Gypsum, Red Peony.
Mince these and decoct them in water for consumption.

Pain-Relieving and Qi-Regulating Decoction
After taking the previous drink for flow of qi, take this prescription.
Ingredients: Perilla Leaves, Magnolia Bark, Dried Tangerine Peel, Fresh Licorice, Pinellia, Radix Notopterygii, Chuanxiong, Fang Feng, White Peony, White Atractylodes, Angelica Sinensis, Yellow Foetid, Anemarrhena, Frankincense, Chai Hu.
Add three slices of ginger and one jujube, decoct and consume without time constraints.

Refined Stone Powder
Treats ear stones that are hard as stone and unchanged in color.
Burned Deer Antler Ash: eight liang; White Licorice: three liang; Coarse Yellow Stone: two jin.
Mix these with five sheng of good vinegar, first burn the stones until red, then quench in vinegar, burn again and quench until the vinegar is used up. Grind to powder and mix with the remaining vinegar to form a paste for application, which will soften the hardened area. Apply it to the roasted area as well.

Collection of Medical Works from Ancient and Modern Times, Volume 137

Ear Section[126p]

　　　　单方

　　耳肿风毒肿起，出血：取柳虫粪化水，取清汁，调白矾末少许，滴之。【《肘后》】
　　聤耳出水：苦竹蛀屑、狼牙、白蔹等分为末，和匀，频掺之。【《圣惠》】
　　耳脓作痛，因水入耳内者：如圣散用箭干内蛀末、腻粉各一钱，麝香五分为末，以绵杖缴尽，送药入耳，以绵塞定。有恶物放令流出。甚者三度必愈。【《普济方》，下同】
　　聤耳出脓水：枣蠹虫屎研末，同麝香少许吹之。
　　蜈蚣入耳：炙猪肪掩耳，自出。

　　百虫入耳：椒末一钱，酢半盏，浸良久，少少滴入自出。【《续千金方》】
　　老人耳聋：猪肾一对去膜，切，以粳米二合、葱白二根、薤白七根、人参二分、防风一分为末，同煮粥食。【《奉亲养老方》】
　　蚰蜒入耳：湿生虫研烂，涂耳边，自出；或摊纸上作捻，安入耳中亦出。【《卫生宝鉴》】
　　肾虚耳聋：用鹿肾一对去脂膜，切，以豉汁入粳米二合煮粥食，亦可作羹。【《圣惠方》】[127p]

Single Prescriptions

Swelling and inflammation of the ear with bleeding: Take the droppings of willow insects, mix with water, extract the clear juice, and add a small amount of powdered alum, then drip it in. [“Zhou Hou”]

Ear discharge with fluid: Mix equal parts of bamboo wormwood, wolf tooth, and white vine into a powder, and apply frequently. [“Sheng Hui”]

Painful ear pus due to water entering the ear: Use a mix of one penny of worm-eaten arrow shaft powder and greasy powder, and five cents of musk, grind together into a powder, use cotton to pack tightly, insert the medicine into the ear, and plug with cotton to secure. Let any foul material flow out. In severe cases, it will heal after three times. [“Pu Ji Fang,” same applies below]

Ear discharge with pus: Grind the droppings of jujube borers, and blow in with a little musk.

Centipede in the ear: Cover the ear with roasted lard, and it will come out by itself.

Various insects in the ear: Use one penny of pepper powder, half a cup of vinegar, soak for a long time, and drip in small amounts to expel. [“Xu Qian Jin Fang”]

Elderly person with deafness: Take a pair of pig kidneys, remove the membrane, slice, and combine with two cups of glutinous rice, two green onions, seven garlic chives, two parts ginseng, and one part fangfeng, grind together, and cook into porridge for consumption. [“Feng Qin Yang Lao Fang”]

Gecko in the ear: Grind moist growth insect into a paste, apply to the ear side, and it will come out; or twist it into a roll on paper, and place it in the ear to also extract. [“Wei Sheng Bao Jian”]

Deafness from kidney deficiency: Use a pair of deer kidneys, remove the fatty membrane, slice, and with fermented soy sauce, mix with two cups of glutinous rice to cook porridge, which can also be made into soup. [“Sheng Hui Fang”][127p]

　　卒耳聋：黄蜡不拘多少，和茯苓末细嚼，茶汤下。 【《普济方》】

Deafness: For deafness, take half a spoonful of goose oil, a small quantity of magnetite, and a little musk. Mix thoroughly, form into a pellet using cotton, and place it in the ear. Hold a small piece of raw iron in the mouth, using three to five pieces for effectiveness.

　　耳鸣耳聋一二十年者：用柘根二十斤，菖蒲五斤，各以水一石，煮取汁五斗，故铁二十斤煅赤，以水五斗浸取清水，合水一石五斗，用米二石，面二斗，如常酿酒成，用真磁石三斤为末，浸酒中三宿，日夜饮之，取醉而眠，闻人声乃止。

For chronic deafness: Take mouse bile, have the patient lie on their side, and drip the bile into the ear until it is finished. After a moment, the bile will flow out from the other ear. Initially, this may worsen the deafness, but after half a day, it will improve. This remedy can treat deafness that has lasted for thirty years. However, mouse bile is hard to obtain; once the mouse dies, the bile quickly dissipates. It may be available around the third day of the third lunar month.

Mouse brain marrow, wrapped in cotton and stuffed in the ear, can also treat deafness.

For ear deafness: Use snake gall to plug the ear; it is remarkably effective.

For deafness due to air blockage: Grind genuine musk into powder, blow it into the ear using a green onion stalk, then plug the ear with green onion; it will restore hearing.

Hearing loss: Take one seed of dadou (castor bean) and remove the heart and skin, take one wingless cicada and remove its wings and legs; combine these two and grind them into a paste, wrap in cotton and plug into the ear. Replace as necessary; this method is very effective.

If the ear suddenly swells and oozes pus, along with both ears and treating hearing loss with pus: Take desiccated alum and grind it finely, then blow a little into the ear with a reed tube three to four times a day; or wrap cotton around a jujube pit and plug the ear. One method involves mixing with table salt and then adding alum powder, which is particularly effective. Another method involves first wrapping a piece of paper to absorb the ear's secretions, then putting in alum powder, and finally adding salt powder; enduring this for a long time will result in healing, usually without needing to repeat. Another method does not use salt. Additionally, take the root of shanglu (a plant) and clean it, then cut it with a bamboo knife to the size of a jujube pit; plug it into the ear, which also treats internal sores.

For pus to flow from the ear: Fire-calcined white alum should be ground into powder, mix in a small amount of musk, and wrap in cotton to plug the ear. [From "Bencao"]

If pus flows from the ear, swelling and pain have subsided but pus continues to flow, use this method mixed with divine efficacy. Use three qian of calcined white alum, two qian of dried carmine, and 1.5 fen of musk, grinding them into an extremely fine powder, stored in an airtight container. When needed, first make a ball of new cotton, squeeze out the pus from the ear, then use damp cotton to roll the medicine and insert it deep into the ear, doing this two to three times daily will lead to self-healing. [From "Wai Ke Zheng Zong"]

Another method: finely grind magnetic stone and wrap it to insert into the deaf ear, separately using iron sand powder to insert into the hearing ear; this will naturally allow hearing. [From "Zhi Zhi"][133p]

For chronic deafness: Obtain turtle urine and drip it into the ear using a green onion stalk. To collect the urine, shine a mirror on the turtle to stimulate urination, or apply moxibustion to its rear to induce urination.

　　聤耳出汁：夜明沙二钱，麝香一字为末，拭净掺之。【《圣惠方》】
　　底耳疼痛：桑螵蛸一个烧存性，麝香一字研末，每用半字掺入神效。有脓先缴净。【经验方。】
　　百虫入耳：小便少少滴之。 【《圣惠方》，下同】
　　劳聋已久：童子小便，乘热少少频滴之。
　　熏耳治聋：蚕退纸作捻，入麝香二钱，入笔管烧烟熏之，三次即开。【《肘后方》】[136p]

  1. When a centipede enters the ear: a small amount of cow's milk drips in and comes out immediately. If it enters the abdomen, drink one or two liters, and it will turn to water.

  2. For pus coming from the ear: half a coin of sea turquoise and a word of musk ground into powder, clean it with cotton, and blow it into the ear.

  3. For ear sores that are swollen and painful: mix powdered galls with cold water, apply wet, then sprinkle dry on it.

  4. For pus coming from the ear: blow powdered galls into it, or use one tael of dried powdered galls and three qian of burnt whole scorpions made into powder, then mix into the ear.

  5. Sudden ear pain: Heat three to five jin of salt, wrap it in blue cloth, and rest your ear on it; if it cools, reheat, and it will be effective immediately.

  6. For fluid discharge from the ear: two qian of night-bright sand and one word of musk ground into powder, clean the ear and sprinkle this mixture.

  7. For ear pain: one preserved sea turquoise, and a word of musk ground into powder, use half a word as a mixture, shows remarkable effect. If there is pus, first clean it out.

  8. For insects entering the ear: drip a small amount of urine into it.

  9. For long-term deafness: a boy's urine, drip a little while warm frequently.

  10. To treat deafness by smoking the ear: take silk paper twisted into a wick, add two qian of musk, smoke it with a pen tube; repeat three times and it will open.[136p]

　　百虫入耳：人乳滴之即出。 【《圣惠方》】
　　多年耳聋，重者用三两度，初起者一上便效：用驴前腿胫骨打破，向日中沥出髓，以瓷盒盛收，每用绵点少许入耳内，侧卧，候药行。其髓不可多用。以白色者为上，黄色者不堪。　　又方：驴前腿胫骨髓，以针沙一合，水二合，浸十日，取清水少许，和髓搅匀，滴少许入耳中。外以新砖一块烧赤泼酢，铺磁石末一两在砖上，枕上至晚，如此三度即通。【《普济方》】
　　塞耳治聋：芫青，巴豆仁、蓖麻仁各一枚，研末，丸枣核大，绵裹塞之。【《圣惠方》】
　　聤耳出脓：蜘蛛一个，胭脂坯子半钱，麝香一字为末，用鹅翎吹之。
　　耳暴聋闭：全蝎去毒为末，酒服一钱，以耳中闻水声即效。【《雅堂杂钞》】
　　脓耳疼痛：蝎梢七枚去毒焙，入麝香半钱为末，挑少许入耳中。日夜三四次，以愈为度。【《杨氏家藏》】[137p]

Insects entering the ear: Apply drops of human milk and they will exit.

For long-term deafness, severe cases require three to two doses; mild cases respond with just one application: Break the shinbone of a donkey's front leg, let the marrow drip out in the sunlight, collect it in a porcelain container, and use a small amount of cotton to place it in the ear. Lie on the side and wait for the medicine to take effect. Do not use too much marrow. The white marrow is the best; yellow marrow is not suitable.

Another method: Take the marrow from the shinbone of a donkey's front leg, mix one part with two parts of water for ten days, then take a little clear water, mix it with the marrow, and drop a small amount into the ear. Burn a piece of new brick until it turns red, pour vinegar over it, and place one tael of powdered magnetic stone on top; pillow your head on it until evening. Repeat this three times for results.

To treat deafness with ear plugs: Use one each of green herb, croton seed, and castor seed, grind into powder, and form into pills the size of jujube pits, wrapping them in cotton.

For ear discharge: Take one spider, half a cash of rouge clay, and a word of musk, grind them together to a powder, and blow it into the ear with a goose feather.

For sudden deafness: Grind whole scorpions after removing their poison, take one qian with wine, and it will be effective when hearing water sounds in the ear.

For painful ear discharge: Take seven tips of scorpions, remove the poison, roast them, then mix with half a qian of musk powdered, and place a small amount into the ear. Repeat day and night three to four times, adjusting according to healing.[137p]

　　物入耳中：以麻纁剪令头散着胶粘上，徐引出之。 【《千金》】
　　百虫入耳：蓝汁、葱汁、韭汁、莴苣汁、鸡冠血、酸酢、香油、稻秆灰汁，俱灌入耳中。【《本草》，下同】　　又方：桃叶挼细塞耳。

　　又方：鲮鲤甲烧灰为末，水调滤过，滴入耳中。

  • For treatment: Burn eel scales to ash and mix with water; filter and drop into the ear.

　　虚损昏聋：大羊尾骨一条，水五碗，煮减半，入葱白五茎，荆芥一握，陈皮一两，面三两，煮熟取汁，搜面作索饼，同羊肉四两，熟和五味食　【《多能鄙事》】
　　暴耳聋者：川椒、巴豆、菖蒲、松脂，以蜡镕为筒子，内耳中，一日一易。或用雄黄一钱，巴豆肉一个，研细，葱涎和作锭子纸卷，塞耳中。或用凌霄花叶杵自然汁，滴耳中。
　　冻耳：用橄榄烧灰，清油调敷；雀脑亦可。
　　冻耳成疮：用柏叶三两，微炙为末，杏仁四十九枚，汤浸去皮，研成膏，乱发两鸡子大，食盐乳香各半两，细研，黄蜡一两五钱，清油一斤。右，先煎油令沸即下乱发，以消尽为度；次下诸药煎，令焦黄，滤去滓，更以绵重滤过，再以慢火煎之；后下乳香、黄蜡等，搅令稠稀得所，于磁器盛。每用鹅翎旋取涂之。　　又方：桕白皮、榆白皮、桑白皮、杏仁汤浸去皮各二两，甘草一两，羊脑髓半斤，俱銼，以羊脑髓煎令黄，滤去滓，于磁器盛，每日用鹅翎蘸药涂之。[140p]

For deafness due to deficiency: Take one sheep's tailbone, five bowls of water, and boil down to half. Add five stalks of green onion, a handful of schizonepeta, one tael of dried tangerine peel, and three taels of flour. Boil until cooked, extract the juice, mix the flour to make dough cakes, and combine with four taels of cooked sheep meat, seasoned with five flavors.

For acute deafness: Use Sichuan pepper, croton, calamus, and pine resin, melted with wax to create a funnel to insert into the ear, changing it daily. Alternatively, mix one qian of realgar with one croton seed, grind finely, and combine with green onion juice to make into a paper roll to plug the ear. Another option is to use the juice from the leaves of the trumpet vine, dropping it into the ear.

For frozen ear: Use ashes from olives mixed with clear oil to apply; bird's brain can also be used.

For frozen ear with sores: Take three taels of cypress leaves, slightly roast and grind them into powder, along with forty-nine almonds soaked in broth, peeled, and ground to paste. Add two chicken eggs in disarray, half a tael of salt, and half a tael of frankincense, finely ground, along with one tael and five qian of yellow wax and one pound of clear oil. First, boil the oil until bubbling, then add the disarrayed materials until dissolved; next, add the prepared powders and boil until golden brown, filtering out the residue multiple times with cotton, and simmer gently again. Finally, incorporate the frankincense and yellow wax, stirring to achieve the desired consistency, and store in a ceramic container. Apply using a goose feather.

Another formula: Use two taels each of the white bark from the mulberry, elm, and apricot, soaked in almond broth to remove the skins; one tael of licorice; and half a jin of sheep's brain marrow, all chopped. Boil the sheep's brain marrow until yellow and filter out the residue, storing in a ceramic container. Use a goose feather daily to dip into the medicine for application.[140p]

　　诸虫入耳：鸡冠血滴入即出。 【《胜金方》】
　　蜒蚰入耳：生油调鸡心血滴入，即出。 【《总录》】

If various insects enter the ear: drop chicken crown blood in and they will come out.

　　聤耳出脓：穿山甲烧存性，入麝香少许吹之，三日，水干即愈。【《鲍氏小儿方》】
　　耳内疼痛：穿山甲三个，夹土狗二个，同炒焦黄为末，每吹一字入耳内，亦治耳聋。【《普济方》】
　　耳鸣耳聋卒聋，及肾虚耳内如风水钟鼓声：穿山甲一大片，以蛤粉炒赤，蝎梢七个，麝香少许为末，以麻油化蜡，和作梃子，绵裹塞之。【《摄生方》】

  • For ear discharge: Take a piece of pangolin, burn it to preserve its essence, add a little musk and blow it in. In three days, when the water is dry, it will heal.

　　《西山经》：符禺之山，有木焉，名曰文茎，其实如枣，可以已聋。

　　　　针灸

　　《素问》曰：暴聋气蒙，耳目不明，取天牖。
　　邪客于手阳明之络，令人耳聋，时不闻音，刺手大指次指爪甲上，去端如韭叶，各一痏，立闻；不已，刺中指爪甲上与肉交者，立闻。其不时闻者，不可刺也。耳中生风者，亦刺之如此数，左刺右，右刺左。　　耳聋刺手阳明，不已，刺其通脉出耳前去者。　　邪客于手足少阴太阴是阳明之络，此五络者皆会于耳中，上络左角。五络俱竭，令人身脉皆动而形无知也，其状若尸，或曰尸厥。刺其足大指内侧爪甲上，去端如韭叶；后刺足心；后刺足中指爪甲上，各一痏；后刺手大指内侧，去端如韭叶；后刺手心主少阴锐骨之端，各一痏，立已；不已，以竹管吹其两耳，鬄其左角之发方一寸，燔治；饮以美酒一杯，不能饮者，灌之立已。[143p]

Translation of the Classical Chinese text:

"The Classic of the Western Mountains: On the mountain of Fuyu, there is a tree named Wenjing, whose fruit is like a jujube and can cure deafness.

In the midst of Yin Mountain, there are many hawthorns, whose leaves resemble those of elm and are square-shaped, and whose fruit is like red beans; eating them can also cure deafness.

Acupuncture

The "Suwen" states: When deafness occurs due to a sudden disturbance, the eyes and ears become unclear; use sky windows.

Pathogenic factors on the Yangming meridian of the hand can cause ear deafness, making one unable to hear sounds. Insert needles into the fingernail of the index finger and the thumb, removing the needle as one would with chive leaves, puncturing each once for effectiveness; if there is no immediate effect, insert into the fingernail of the middle finger where it meets the flesh for immediate effect. If there is still no response, do not insert again. If wind is generated in the ear, use the same method of puncturing several times, moving from left to right, then right to left. To alleviate ear deafness through the Yangming meridian, if not resolved, puncture the pathway leading to the front of the ear.

Pathogenic factors affecting the Taiyin and Shaoyin of the hands and feet are related to the Yangming meridian; these five meridians all converge in the ear, with connections to the left angle. When all five meridians become blocked, it causes the body’s qi to stir, leaving one in a state of unawareness, resembling a corpse, or some may say, a state of corpse-like stupor. Puncture the inner side of the toenail of the big toe, leaving it punctured as one would with chive leaves; then puncture the center of the foot; next, puncture the toenail of the middle toe, each once; then puncture the inner side of the thumb, as one would with chive leaves; finally, puncture the heart point of the Shaoyin where the sharp bone ends, each once, for immediate effect; if still unresolved, blow into both ears with a bamboo tube, take one inch of hair from the left angle, burn it, and drink a cup of fine wine. If one cannot drink, administer it forcefully for immediate effect."[143p]

　　肝病者，虚则目(目巟)(目巟)无所见，耳无所闻，善恐，如人将捕之，取其经厥阴与少阳，气逆则头痛耳聋不聪颊肿，取血者。　　肺病者虚则少气，不能报息，耳聋嗌干，取其经太阴足太阳之外、厥阴内血者。　　《灵枢经》云：人之耳中鸣者，何气使然？岐伯曰：耳者宗脉之所聚也。故胃中空则宗脉虚，虚则下溜，脉有所竭者，故耳鸣。补客主人，手大指爪甲上，与肉交者也。　　又云：上气不足，耳为之苦鸣，补足外踝下留之。[144p]

Individuals with liver disease, when deficient, cannot see with their eyes or hear with their ears, are often fearful, as if someone is about to catch them. One should treat using the channels of Jueyin and Shaoyang; if the qi is rebellious, symptoms include headaches, deafness, and facial swelling, and one should draw blood.

For those with lung disease, if deficient, there is shortness of breath, an inability to exhale fully, deafness, and a dry throat; one should treat using the channels of Taiyin, on the foot of Shaoyang externally, and Jueyin internally to draw blood.

The "Lingshu" states: When there is ringing in the ears, what qi causes this? Qibo replied: The ears are where the ancestral vessels gather. Therefore, when the stomach is empty, the ancestral vessels become deficient, and if deficient, they flow downwards, leading to a deficiency in the vessels, hence the ringing in the ears. Nourish both the host and the guest; it is at the junction of the thumb's nail and flesh.

Furthermore, it is said: When there is insufficient upward qi, the ears suffer from distressing ringing; nourish it at the location below the outer ankle.[144p]

　　又云：髓海不足，则脑转耳鸣，审守其输，调其虚实。　　又云：手太阳之筋，其病肩髀引颈而痛，耳中鸣，其痛转筋者，治在燔针劫刺之，以知为度，以痛为输。　　手太阳之脉所生病者，耳聋目黄颊肿，视盛虚热寒陷下调之也。　　热病身重，骨痛，耳聋而好瞑，取之骨，以第四针，五十九刺。骨病不食，啮齿耳青，索骨于肾，不得索之土，士者脾也。　　《甲乙经》曰：手太阳厥逆耳聋，治主病者。　　耳中有干擿，禁不可灸。
　　耳门耳中有脓，禁不可灸。
　　颈痛项不得顾，耳目不明，风池主之。　　肩背痛暴聋，气蒙耳目不开，天牖主之。　　热病汗不出，耳鸣聋无所闻，阳谷主之。　　耳聋鸣，窍阴主之。
　　暴病头痛身热痛，肌肉动耳聋，束骨主之。　　头风耳后痛，完骨主之。[145p]

It is also said: When the marrow sea is deficient, the brain turns and the ears ring. Carefully observe the flow and regulate the deficiency and excess. It is also said: The hand's sun channel affects the shoulder, hip, and neck, causing pain and ringing in the ears. If the pain twists the muscles, treatment lies in the moxibustion and needling based on knowledge and pain. Diseases arising from the hand's sun meridian manifest as deafness, yellowing of the eyes, and swollen cheeks. Adjust for excessive heat or cold that is deficient and sinking. In cases of febrile illness with heaviness, bone pain, deafness, and desire for sleep, target the bones with the fourth needle, using fifty-nine punctures. Bone ailments that prevent eating, with enamel-like ears deepening to green, seek the bones in the kidneys, but refrain from drawing from the earth; scholars correspond to the spleen. The "Jia Yi Classic" states: Hand sun counterflow causes deafness; treat the root of the issue. If there is dryness in the ears, do not apply moxibustion.

If there is pus in the ear canal, do not apply moxibustion.

For neck pain and inability to turn, with unclear vision, the wind pool controls it. Severe shoulder and back pain leading to sudden deafness, with obstructed hearing and vision, the heavenly window regulates it. In cases of fever where sweat does not emerge, resulting in ringing in the ears and deafness, the yang valley controls it.

Deafness and ringing in the ears are managed by the lower orifice.

In sudden illness with headache and body heat, muscle twitching leads to deafness; the bound bone controls it. For a headache with pain behind the ears, the completed bone regulates it.[145p]

　　癫疾多言耳鸣，实则聋，偏历主之。　　耳鸣，取耳前动脉。
　　聋而不痛，取足少阳；聋而痛，取手阳明。　　耳鸣，百会及颔厌、颅息、天窻、大陵、偏历、前谷、后溪皆主之。　　耳痛聋鸣，上关主之，刺不可深。
　　耳聋鸣，下关及阳溪、关冲、液门、阳谷主之。　　耳聋鸣，头颔痛，耳门主之。
　　头重颔痛，引耳中，憹憹嘈嘈，和髎主之。　　聋耳中癫溲，癫溲者，若风，听会主之。　　耳聋填填如无闻，憹憹嘈嘈若蝉鸣，頞颊鸣，听宫主之。下颊取之，譬如破声刺此。　　聋，翳风及会宗、下关关　原作「空」，据《甲乙》卷十二手太阳少阳脉动发耳病第五改。主之。　　耳聋无闻，天窗窗　原作「空」，据《甲乙》卷十二手太阳少阳脉动发耳病第五改。主之。　　耳聋嘈嘈无所闻，天容主之。
　　耳鸣无闻，肩贞及完骨主之。
　　耳中生风，耳鸣耳聋时不闻，商阳主之。　　聋及耳中不通，合谷主之。[146p]

The condition of deafness often involves complaints of tinnitus, yet in reality, it is a form of deafness governed by the Pathway of the Fen. Tinnitus is linked to the arterial movement in front of the ear.

For deafness without pain, focus on the Lesser Yang at the foot; for deafness with pain, the Yangming at the hand is indicated. Tinnitus is governed by points like Baihui, Yanyan, Lusi, Tiankuang, Daling, Pianli, Qianggu, and Houxi. Ear pain with deafness is related to Shangguan, with the admonition to not pierce deeply.

For deafness and tinnitus, the points Xiaguan alongside Yangxi, Guanchong, Yumen, and Yanggu should be considered. If deafness and tinnitus coincide with pain in the head or jaw, the point Ermen is significant.

Should there be heaviness in the head and pain in the jaw, drawing to the ear, with sounds like chirping or buzzing, the Hejiao point is of relevance.

In cases of deafness with sounds resembling wind or frenzy in the ear, the Tinghui point should be applied. If there is an emptiness in hearing that feels as if nothing is heard, leading to a continuous noise akin to cicadas, the Tingong point should be noted, with the emphasis on the lower jaw much like a broken sound piercing through this condition.

For deafness without hearing, focus on the Tianshu point. If there is clamor without discernible hearing, Tiansheng is the place of focus.

When wind arises within the ear, leading to both tinnitus and deafness during non-hearing times, focus on the Shangyang point. For conditions of deafness and blockage within the ear, the Hegu point is to be utilized.[146p]

　　耳聋两颞颥痛，中渚主之。
　　耳浑浑焞焞无所闻，外关主之。
　　卒气聋，四渎主之。
　　《千金方》曰：耳痛，耳聋嘈嘈，上关、下关、四白、百会、颅息、翳风、耳门、颔厌、天窻、阳溪、关冲、液门、中渚。　　耳聋嘈嘈若蝉鸣，天容、听会、听宫。　　耳暴聋，天牖、四渎。
　　耳前痛，少商。
　　耳痛，曲池。
　　浑浑焞焞，聋无所闻，外关、会宗。　　耳鸣，前谷、后溪。仍取偏历，大陵。　　颔痛引耳，嘈嘈耳鸣无闻，腕骨、阳谷、肩贞、窍阴、侠溪。　　风聋鸣，商阳，刺入一分，留一呼，灸三壮，左取右，右取左，如食顷。　　《医学纲目》曰：耳聋耳鸣，或疼或痒，或聤耳，听会主之。穴在耳珠前陷中，泻八吸。　　翳风针入半寸，泻七吸；或合谷，或三里。　　又法：翳风在耳前陷后，按之引耳中，令病人先以钱二十四文，口咬侧卧，取之针透，令病人闭口摇头，其怒气从耳出。　　听会、中渚、临泣，针法如前。[147p]

Deafness with pain in both temples is managed by the point Zhongzhu.

When hearing is muddled and there is no sound perception, the point Waiguan is used.

For sudden deafness, the points Sidu are applicable.

The "Thousand Gold Recipe" states: for ear pain or deafness with a buzzing sound, use the points Shangguan, Xiaguang, Sibai, Baihui, Luxi, Yifeng, Ermen, Hanyan, Tiankuang, Yangxi, Guanchong, Yumen, and Zhongzhu. Deafness with a buzzing sound like that of cicadas can be addressed with points Tianrong, Tinghui, and Tinggong.

For sudden deafness, use Tianyou and Sidu.

For pain in front of the ear, the point Shaoshang is indicated.

For ear pain, use Quqi.

When hearing is muddled and there is total deafness, apply the points Waiguan and Huizong. For tinnitus, the points Qiangu and Houxi should be considered. Additionally, apply Pieli and Daling.

For ear pain radiating to the ear, with a buzzing sound where there is no hearing, consider Wangu, Yanggu, Jianzheng, Qiaoyin, and Xiaxi.

For wind-related deafness buzzing, utilize Shangyang, inserting a needle to a depth of one portion, leaving one breath, and moxibustion three times. Alternate sides as if eating.

The "Medical Guidelines" states: for deafness and tinnitus, with either pain or itchiness, or a feeling of fullness, use the point Tinghui. The acupoint is located in the depression at the front of the ear lobe, apply eight draining and suction techniques.

For the point Yifeng, insert the needle half an inch deep with seven draining and suction techniques; you may also use Hegu or Sanli.

Another method: Yifeng is located in the depression before the ear, pressing it helps draw the sensation inward. Instruct the patient to first hold twenty-four coins in their mouth while lying on their side and use needles to pierce, asking the patient to keep their mouth closed and shake their head, releasing the anger through the ear.

For the points Tinghui, Zhongzhu, and Linqi, use the same needle technique as previously mentioned.[147p]

　　耳虚鸣，肾俞、太溪。
　　灸耳暴聋，苍朮长七分，一头切平，一头削尖，将尖头插耳中，于平头上灸七壮，重者二七壮，觉耳内热即效。　　《景岳全书》曰：风聋，灸上星七壮，令气通耳中，即愈。　　耳聋痛，翳风，灸七壮。
　　耳聋，合谷灸七壮；或外关、听宫、肾俞、偏历。　　《东医宝鉴》曰：耳鸣，取液门、耳门、中渚、上关、完骨、临泣、阳谷、前谷、后溪、阳溪、偏历、合谷、大陵、太溪、金门。　　耳聋，取中渚、外关、和髎、听会、听宫、合谷、商阳、中冲。

　　《养性书》曰：以手摩耳轮，不拘遍数。所谓修其城郭，以补肾气，以防聋聩也。　　养耳力者常饱。[148p]

Ear buzzing and ringing can be treated at the points of Shen Shu and Tai Xi.

For sudden deafness, use a moxa stick on the ear with the herb Atractylodes, cut into seven parts—one end flat and the other pointed. Insert the pointed end into the ear and moxa the flat end for seven times; if the condition is severe, do it for fourteen times. When you feel heat inside the ear, it is effective. The "Complete Book of Jing Yue" says that for wind-related deafness, moxa seven times at the point Shang Xing to allow the qi to flow into the ear, which can lead to recovery.

For ear deafness and pain, use moxa seven times. For deafness, moxa at He Gu point seven times; or at Wai Guan, Ting Gong, Shen Shu, and Pian Li. The "Treasure Mirror of Eastern Medicine" states that for ear buzzing, select points such as Ye Men, Er Men, Zhong Zhu, Shang Guan, Wan Gu, Lin Qi, Yang Gu, Qian Gu, Hou Xi, Yang Xi, Pian Li, He Gu, Da Ling, Tai Xi, and Jin Men.

For ear deafness, use points Zhong Zhu, Wai Guan, He Liao, Ting Hui, Ting Gong, He Gu, Shang Yang, and Zhong Chong.

Regarding guidance, the "Book of Nurturing Life" suggests massaging the ear rim without limitation on the number of times. This is to strengthen kidney qi and prevent deafness. To maintain hearing strength, one should always feel full.[148p]

　　《保生秘要》曰：定息以坐塞兑，咬紧牙关，以脾肠二指捏紧鼻孔，睁二目，使气串耳通窍，内觉哄哄有声，行之二三日，窍通为度。　　时常将两耳返听于归元取静，或存息闭口鼻气，意想从耳出，又收返听，耳自然聪。耳病凡搓掌心五十度，热闭耳门空观，次又搓又闭又观，如此六度，耳重皆然，兼以后功，无不应验。　　用意推散其火，男则逆收藏于两肾间，女则逆归于两乳下，或耳中。或按耳门，内若蝉鸣，咽津液降气，自安。　　耳痛，想火烧两肾，又升肾水洗之，或按耳户，使鸣数次，咽津液，气下即安。　　耳病以意散其火，逆归藏于两肾内，或耳中有物，即以意取出之。　　《景岳全书》曰：凡耳窍或损或塞，或震伤，以致暴聋，或鸣不止者，即宜以手中指于耳窍中轻轻按捺，随捺随放，随放随捺，或轻轻摇动，以引其气。捺之数次，其气必至，气至则窍自通矣。凡值此者，若不速为导引，恐因而渐闭，而竟至不开耳。[149p]

The "Secrets of Preserving Life" states: Engage in deep breathing to block distractions, clench your teeth, press your nostrils tightly with two fingers, and open your eyes wide, allowing your breath to connect your ears and clear your passages. You may feel a buzzing sound inside; practice this for two or three days until your passages are open. Regularly listen with both ears in order to return to a quiet state. You can also hold your breath, closing your mouth and nostrils, and imagine the breath coming out of your ears, then draw your focus back; your ears will naturally become sharp. For ear ailments, rub the palms of your hands together fifty times, applying heat to the ear to open it, and continue this rubbing and observing for six repetitions. Symptoms will improve, and with ongoing practice, results will be evident. Use mental focus to disperse heat; for men, gather it back between the kidneys, and for women, draw it back beneath the breasts or to the ears. You can press the ear area, and if you hear a buzzing, swallow saliva to calm the energy within.

For ear pain, visualize fire burning the kidneys, and cleanse it with kidney water; press the ear several times to stimulate sound, swallow saliva, and breathe down until you feel at ease. For ear problems, use your mind to scatter the heat, drawing it back and storing it within the kidneys, or if something is lodged in the ear, mentally remove it.

The "Complete Works of Jing Yue" states: If the ear passages are damaged, blocked, or injured, leading to sudden deafness or persistent buzzing, gently press your fingertip against the ear opening, pushing and releasing in rhythm. This should be done several times; the air will flow, and when it does, the passage will naturally open. If these conditions occur, failing to take timely action may result in gradual blockage, ultimately leading to complete ear closure.[149p]

　　　　医案

　　《丹铅续录》云：王万里时患耳痛，魏文靖公劝以服青盐、鹿茸煎雄附为剂。且言此药非为虚损服之，曷不观《易》之坎为耳，坎水藏在肾，开窍于耳，在志为恐，恐则伤肾，故为耳痛。气阳运动常显，血阴流行常幽。血在形如水在天地间，故坎为血卦，是经中已着病证矣。竟饵之而良愈。
　　沈存中云：予为河北察访使时，病赤目四十余日，黑睛旁黯赤成疮，昼夜痛楚，百疗不瘥。郎官丘革相见，问予病目如此，曾耳中痒否？若耳中痒，即是肾家风。有四生散疗肾风，每作二三服即瘥，闾里号为圣散子。予传其方合服之，午时一服，临卧一服，目反大痛，至二鼓时乃能眠，及觉目赤稍散，不复痛矣，更进三四服，遂平安如常。是时孙和甫学士帅镇，闻予说，大喜曰：吾知所以自治目矣。向久病目，尝见吕吉甫参政云：顷目病久不瘥，因服透冰丹乃瘥。如其言修合透冰丹一剂，试服了二三十服，目遂愈，乃知透冰丹亦疗肾风耳。[150p]

Medical Case

According to "Danqian Xulu," Wang Wanli suffered from ear pain at that time. Wei Wenjing Gong advised him to take a potion made of blue salt and deer antler decoction. He mentioned that this medicine was not for consumption due to deficiency, and asked why one shouldn’t consider the "I Ching," where "Kan" corresponds to the ear. The Kan water resides in the kidney, opening the orifice at the ear. In terms of emotion, it relates to fear; fear injures the kidney, hence the ear pain. The movement of Qi Yang is always evident, while the flow of Blood Yin is often hidden. Blood, like water between heaven and earth, leads to Kan being the hexagram of blood, indicating disease is already documented in the classics. In the end, after taking it, he was cured.

Shen Cunzhong stated: When I was an inspection official in Hebei, I suffered from red eyes for more than forty days. The black part of my eyes was darkened and developed sores, causing pain day and night. Various treatments failed to heal me. The gentleman Qiu Ge, upon seeing my condition, asked if my ears had been itchy. If they were itchy, it would indicate kidney wind. There is a formula called Si Sheng San to treat kidney wind, and it typically takes two or three doses to heal, known locally as the "sacred powder." I transmitted the formula and took it as directed: one dose at noon and one before sleeping. My eyes began to hurt greatly, and I could only sleep at the second watch; upon waking, my eyes had slightly improved and were no longer painful. After taking three or four more doses, I returned to normal health. At that time, Scholar Sun Hefu was in charge and, upon hearing me, was overjoyed, saying: "I now know how to treat the eyes myself." Earlier, suffering from a long-term eye ailment, I once heard Lu Jifu, a political advisor, say that after a prolonged eye illness, he healed himself by taking the Tou Bing Dan (Icing Pill). Following his recommendation, I tried taking two or three dozen doses, and my eyes were cured, leading me to realize that the Tou Bing Dan also treats kidney wind in the ears.[150p]

　　《圣惠》曰：有人耳痒，一日一作，可畏，直挑剔出血稍愈。此乃肾脏虚，致浮毒上攻，未易以常法治也，宜服透冰丹，勿饮酒啖湿面蔬菜鸡猪之属，能尽一月为佳，不能戒无效。
　　《墨客挥犀》：虫之类能入耳者，不独蜒蚰，如壁虱、萤火、叩头虫、皂荚虫皆能入耳为害。余有外亲曾为虫入耳，自谓必死，乃极家其所有恣情耗荡，凡数年，家业遂破。虫出疾愈，验之，乃叩头虫也。又有人为蜒蚰入耳，遇其极时，不觉以头撞柱，至血流不知，云痒甚不可忍。蜒蚰入耳，往往食髓，至冬又能滋生。凡虫入耳者，惟用生油灌之为妙。[151p]

"The Sacred Benefit" states: If someone experiences itchy ears that occur daily, it is a cause for concern. Poking at it until it bleeds may bring slight relief. This indicates kidney deficiency, leading to a floating toxin ascending, which is not easily treated by conventional methods. It is advisable to take 'Ice-Clear Pill' and avoid alcohol and damp vegetables, chicken, and pork for at least a month for the best results; if one cannot abstain, treatment will be ineffective.

"Notes from Ink Visitors": Creatures that can enter the ear are not just earwigs; such as wall lice, fireflies, head-banging bugs, and soap pods can also cause harm. I have a distant relative who had a bug enter his ear, convinced he would surely die, and thus squandered his family's resources over several years, leading to his financial ruin. When the bug came out, he discovered it was a head-banging bug. Another individual had an earwig enter his ear; in a peak moment of distress, he unconsciously banged his head against a pillar, causing him to bleed without realizing it, claiming the itch was unbearable. Earwigs often consume marrow and can breed in the winter. For any bug in the ear, the best remedy is to flush it out with raw oil.[151p]

　　《薛己医案》曰：先君尝睡间，有虫入耳，痛瞀。将生姜擦猫鼻，其尿自出，取尿滴耳内，虫即出而愈。　　百户张锦谓予曰：耳内生疮，不时作痛，痛而欲死，痛止如故，诊其脉皆安静，予谓非疮也。话间痛忽作，予度其有虫入耳，令回，急取猫尿滴耳，果出一臭虫，遂不复痛。或用麻油滴之，则虫死难出。或用炒芝麻枕之，则虫亦出，但俱不及猫尿之速也。
　　文选姚海山耳根赤肿，寒热作痛，此属三焦风热也。但中气素虚，以补中益气，加山栀、炒黄芩、牛蒡子治之而愈。
　　一儒者因怒耳内作痛出水，或用祛风之剂，筋挛作痛，肢体如束，此肝火伤血也，用六味丸料，数服愈。[152p]

The "Medical Cases of Xue Ji" states: The late emperor once had a bug crawl into his ear while sleeping, causing intense pain. He took ginger and rubbed it on a cat's nose, and its urine came out. He then dripped that urine into his ear, and the bug came out, resulting in a cure. Zhang Jin, a hundred households, said to me: When there is a sore in the ear that causes periodic severe pain, one may feel as though they want to die, yet when the pain subsides, it feels the same as before, and upon diagnosing the pulse, all seems calm. I deduced it was not a sore. Suddenly, the pain arose, and I suspected a bug had entered the ear. I instructed him to turn back, quickly took the cat's urine and dripped it into the ear, which caused a stinky bug to come out, and thereafter there was no more pain. Some use hemp oil to drip in, but the bug dies and is hard to remove. Others use fried sesame to treat it, and the bug also comes out, but neither method is as quick as using cat urine.

Wen Xuan’s Yao Haishan had a red swollen ear root with cold and hot pains, indicating wind heat from the sanjiao. However, with pre-existing deficiency of the central qi, I added Gardenia fruit, fried Scutellaria, and Burdock seed to tonify the middle and benefit qi, and he recovered.

A scholar, due to anger, experienced pain in the ear accompanied by fluid discharge. Using wind-dispersing medicine caused muscle spasms and pain, and limbs felt constrained. This was a result of liver fire injuring the blood. I used the Six Flavor Pill, and after several doses, he recovered.[152p]

　　举人毛石峰子年二十，耳内出水或作痛，年余矣，脉洪数，左尺益甚。此属肝肾二经虚热也，用加减八味丸料一剂而愈。
　　一男子每入房，耳内或作痒，或出水，常以银簪探入，甚喜阴凉。此属肾经热也，用加减八味丸而愈。
　　一妇人因怒发热，每经行即两耳出脓，两太阳作痛，以手按之痛稍止，怒则胸胁乳房胀痛，或寒热往来，或小便频数，或小腹胀闷。此皆属肝火血虚也，先用栀子清肝散二剂，又用加味逍遥散数剂，诸证悉退；又以补中益气加五味而全愈。
　　一妇人经行后，因怒气劳役，即发寒热，耳内作痛。余以经行为血虚，用八珍汤加柴胡；怒气为肝火，用加味逍遥散；劳役为气伤，用补中益气汤加山栀而愈。
　　一妇人耳内作痛，或肿焮，寒热发热。面色素青黄，经行则变赤。余以为怒气伤肝，郁结伤脾，用加味归脾汤、加味逍遥散而愈。[153p]

A scholar, Mao Shifeng, at the age of twenty, experienced water discharge or pain in his ear for over a year. His pulse was rapid and strong, especially at the left wrist. This was attributed to the deficiency heat of the liver and kidney. A dose of the modified Eight-Flavor Pill cured him.

A man would feel itching or experience a discharge in his ear every time he entered a room. He often probed with a silver hairpin, finding great pleasure in the coolness. This was attributed to heat in the kidney channel. He was cured with the modified Eight-Flavor Pill.

　　一妇人耳内肿痛，寒热口苦，耳内出水，焮连颈项，饮食少思。此肝火甚而伤脾也，用小柴胡汤加山栀、牡丹皮，稍愈；用加味逍遥散及八珍汤，加柴胡、山栀、牡丹皮，调补肝脾而全愈。
　　一孀妇，或耳内外作痛，或项侧结核，内热晡热，月经不调，唾痰少食，胸膈不利。余以为郁怒伤肝脾，朝用归脾汤以解脾郁，生脾气；夕用加味逍遥散，以清肝火，生肝血而愈。
　　太卿魏庄渠，癸卯仲冬，耳内作痛，左尺洪大而濇。余曰：此肾水枯竭，不能生肝木，当滋化源。彼不信，仍杂用兼补之剂。余谓其婿陆时若曰：庄渠不能生肾水，来春必不能起。至明年季春十八日，复请治。昏愦不语，颐耳之分已有脓矣，且卵缩便数，方信余言。求治辞不克，用六味丸料壹锺，阴茎舒出，小便十减六七，神思顿醒。余曰：若砭脓出，庶延数日，为立嗣之计，否则脓从耳出，死立待矣。或谓不砭可生者，余因辞归。翌日果耳内出脓，至二十一日己未火日而卒。[154p]

A woman had swelling and pain in her ear, experiencing chills and fever, with a bitter taste in her mouth, ear discharge, and a hot sensation radiating to her neck, along with reduced appetite and thought. A widow had pain in her ear, or exterior ear pain, or a hard lump on the side of her neck, with internal heat characterized by afternoon fevers, irregular menstruation, little saliva and phlegm, and hindered chest. Taiqing Wei Zhuang Qu, in the winter of the year Gui Mao, had ear pain, with the left pulse being large and slippery. I said: this is due to kidney essence depletion, unable to nourish the liver wood, so it is necessary to moisten the source of transformation. He did not believe this and continued to mix other tonifying medicines. I told his son-in-law Lu Shi Ruo that if Zhuang Qu could not nourish kidney essence, he would surely not survive until spring.
